the Federal Open Market Committee on Meeting of January 30-31, 2018

Board of Governors of the Federal Reserve System in Washington, D.C., A joint meeting of the Federal Open Market Committee and the Board of Governors was held in the offices of the on Tuesday, January 30, 2018, at 10:00 a.m. and continued on Wednesday, January 31, 2018, at 9:00 a.m.
